mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*} Q_1 &amp;= 10^{-8}\ C, \\ Q_2 &amp;= -2 \cdot 10^{-8}\ C, \\ \boldsymbol{r}_1 &amp;= \boldsymbol{0}, \\ \boldsymbol{r}_2 &amp;= 0.5\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}}, \\ \boldsymbol{r}_t &amp;= 0.2\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\[1.5ex] \boldsymbol{r}_{t1} &amp;= 0.2\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ |\boldsymbol{r}_{t1}| &amp;= 0.2\ m, \\ \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t1}} &amp;= \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\[1.5ex] \boldsymbol{r}_{t2} &amp;= -0.5\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + 0.2\ m\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ |\boldsymbol{r}_{t2}| &amp;= \frac{\sqrt{29}}{10}\ m, \\ \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t2}} &amp;= -\frac{5 \sqrt{29}}{29}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + \frac{2 \sqrt{29}}{29}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\[1.5ex] \boldsymbol{E}_1 &amp;= k_e \frac{Q_1}{|\boldsymbol{r}_{t1}|^2} \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t1}} \\ &amp;= 2250\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ \boldsymbol{E}_2 &amp;= k_e \frac{Q_2}{|\boldsymbol{r}_{t2}|^2} \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t2}} \\ &amp;= -\frac{18000}{29}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{r}_{t2}} \\ &amp;= \frac{90000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} - \frac{36000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ &amp;\approx 576.3\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} - 230.52\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ \boldsymbol{E} &amp;= \boldsymbol{E}_1 + \boldsymbol{E}_2 \\ &amp;= \frac{90000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + \left(2250 - \frac{36000 \sqrt{29}}{841}\right)\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ &amp;\approx 576.3\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{x}} + 2019.48\ NC^{-1}\ \boldsymbol{\hat{y}}, \\ |\boldsymbol{E}| &amp;\approx 2100.1\ NC^{-1}. \end{align*} </annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" fence="true">]</mo></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">.</mi></mrow></mstyle></mtd></mtr></mtable><annotation encoding="application/x-tex"> \begin{align*}  \lambda &amp;= \frac{dq}{dl} \implies dq = \lambda\ dl = \lambda\ dy, \\  r &amp;= \sqrt{y^2 + s^2}, \\  d|\boldsymbol{E}| &amp;= k_e \frac{dq}{r^2} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \frac{dy}{y^2 + s^2}, \\  d E_x &amp;= \cos \alpha_1\ d|\boldsymbol{E}|, \\  d E_y &amp;= \sin \alpha_1\ d|\boldsymbol{E}|, \\  \cos \alpha_1 &amp;= \frac{s}{r}, \\  \sin \alpha_1 &amp;= -\sin \alpha_2 = -\frac{y}{r}, \\  d E_x &amp;= k_e \lambda s \frac{dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}}, \\  E_x &amp;= k_e \lambda s \int_{-h}^{l - h} \frac{dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}} \\  &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \left[\frac{y}{\sqrt{y^2 + s^2}}\right]_{-h}^{l - h} \\  &amp;= \frac{k_e \lambda}{s} \left[\frac{l - h}{\sqrt{(l - h)^2 + s^2}} + \frac{h}{\sqrt{h^2 + s^2}}\right], \\  d E_y &amp;= k_e \lambda \frac{y\ dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}}, \\  E_y &amp;= -k_e \lambda \int_{-h}^{l - h} \frac{y\ dy}{(y^2 + s^2)^{\frac{3}{2}}} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \left[\frac{1}{\sqrt{y^2 + s^2}}\right]_{-h}^{l - h} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \left[\frac{1}{\sqrt{y^2 + s^2}}\right]_{-h}^{l - h} \\  &amp;= k_e \lambda \left[\frac{1}{\sqrt{(l - h)^2 + s^2}} - \frac{1}{\sqrt{h^2 + s^2}}\right]. \\ \end{align*}
